***argusogen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:argusogen.html>argusogen</a> (109590)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:argusogen.html>argusogen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">argusoog</i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:argusogen.html>argusogen</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">mv</span>

***aristocratie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aristocratie.html>aristocratie</a> (52448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:aristocratie.html>aristocratie</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀριστοκρατίᾱ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aristokratíā</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">aristocracy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> but literally meaning “government by the best”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aristocratie.html>aristocratie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aristocratie.html>aristocratieën</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">aristocraties</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aristocratie.html>aristocratietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>an aristocracy, as form of government, ruling nobilty or first estate
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:adel.html>adel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An esteemed elite
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>Nooit</a> geadelde <a href = vnd.unilang:componisten.html>componisten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> Bach <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Beethoven <a href = vnd.unilang:behoren.html>behoren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onbetwist.html>onbetwiste</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aristocratie.html>aristocratie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muziek.html>muziek</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">never ennobled composers like Bach and Beethoven belong to the undoubted elite of music</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arme.html>arme</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poor person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the 18th century in this form, but attested since the 17th century in a different form.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:armoedzaaier.html>armoedzaaier</a> (22328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:armoede.html>armoede</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poverty; strife</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">zaaier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one who sows</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">earmoedsaaier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">aggressive, argumentative person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. West Frisian <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> borrowed the sense “destitute person” from Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:armoedzaaier.html>armoedzaaier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:armoedzaaiers.html>armoedzaaiers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:armoedzaaier.html>armoedzaaiertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***armpit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:armpit.html>armpit</a> (55124)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">armpitt</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">arme-pitt</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">armput</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">arm</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:armpit.html>armpit</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">armpits</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The cavity beneath the junction of the arm and shoulder.</li>
<li>Somewhere or something considered unpleasant or undesirable.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:armpit.html>armpit</a></b> of America</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">cavity beneath the junction of the arm and shoulder</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">axilla</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">oxter</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">underarm</span>; <span class="Latn" lang="en">armhole</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">now UK dialect</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
</body>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:aron.html>aron</a></i> (also <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">arum</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄρον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">áron</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

***arrenslee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:arrenslee.html>arrenslee</a> (95686)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">narrenslee</i> (<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nar.html>nar</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>slee</a></i>) through <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/apheresis_(linguistics)" class="extiw" title="w:apheresis (linguistics)">aphaeresis</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>Later</a> reinterpreted as a compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ar</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>slee</a></i>, but the former element <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in fact a back-formation from this word.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arrenslee.html>arrenslee</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arrenslee.html>arrensleeën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arrenslee.html>arrensleetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>horse-sleigh</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">ar</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***arrestatie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:arrestatie.html>arrestatie</a> (4001)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">arrestation</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arresteren.html>arresteren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-atie</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***arresteren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:arresteren.html>arresteren</a> (1872)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">aresteren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">arester</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stay, <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arresteren.html>arresteren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to arrest</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanhouden.html>aanhouden</a></span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> ars (15296)</h1><br></body> 
***arse.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a> (66048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">ars</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:ers.html>ers</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ærs</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ears</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*arsaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aars.html>aars</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Arsch</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃érsos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">backside, buttocks</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Julius_Pokorny" class="extiw" title="w:Julius Pokorny">Julius Pokorny</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carl_Darling_Buck" class="extiw" title="w:Carl Darling Buck"><a href = vnd.unilang:carl.html>Carl</a> Darling Buck</a>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">arses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">current in<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/South_Africa" class="extiw" title="w:South Africa">South Africa</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated  in  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_England" class="extiw" title="w:New England">New England</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> now vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The buttocks or more specifically, the <a href = vnd.unilang:anus.html>anus</a>.
<ul><li><b>1485</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Malory" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Malory">Thomas Malory</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://quod.lib.umich.edu/c/cme/MaloryWks2/1:14.3?rgn=div2;view=fulltext">chapter iij</a>, in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Le_Morte_d%27Arthur" class="extiw" title="w:Le Morte d | Arthur">Le <a href = vnd.unilang:morte.html>Morte</a> Darthur</a></i>, book XII:
<dl><dd>amp; thenne he <a href = vnd.unilang:rode.html>rode</a> after the bore / amp; thenne syre laūcelot <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ware.html>ware</a> where the bore set his <b>ars</b> to a tree by an hermytage / Thenne <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a> launcelot ranne atte bore with his spere / amp; ther with the bore torned hym nemly</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, James Smart, <i>The Guardian</i>, 12 March:
<dl><dd>As the novel progresses, he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> shot in the hand with his own gun, shot in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></b> with someone else's and lacerated by a prosthetic weed trimmer.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stupid, mean or despicable person.
<ul><li><b>2007</b>, Martin Harrison, <i>The Judgement of Paris</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=CAlzbwNRMtACamp;pg=PA282amp;dq=%22an+arse%22+-intitle:%22arse%7Carses%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=Rxu5Tt_6EMvrmAWXx_3pBwamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22an%20arse%22%20-intitle%3A%22arse%7Carses%22amp;f=false">p.282</a>:
<dl><dd>“You're an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></b>,” <a href = vnd.unilang:ellen.html>Ellen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a>.  |  “Please? You must like something about <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>  | ?”  |  “I do. You're an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></b>. I just <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> you that. I feel comfy with you, because you're such an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></b>.”</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2007</b>, L. A. Wilson, <i>The Silurian: Book One: The Fox and the Bear</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=vQ24oPwy0LICamp;pg=PA103amp;dq=%22an+arse%22+-intitle:%22arse%7Carses%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=cR-5TrnDAYaGmQW2j92PCAamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22an%20arse%22%20-intitle%3A%22arse%7Carses%22amp;f=false">p.103</a>:
<dl><dd>He looked at <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> just about to call <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></b>, when I <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> him, “You throw it too hard. Try and think of the javelin hitting the target before you throw it. Let it all go through your mind first, see it, feel it, then throw it.”  |  “Good advice, you <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></b>,” he <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> and tried again.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2011</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:joe.html>Joe</a> Abercrombie, <i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:heroes.html>Heroes</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=bVg7laP0XykCamp;pg=PT283amp;dq=%22an+arse%22+-intitle:%22arse%7Carses%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=cR-5TrnDAYaGmQW2j92PCAamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22an%20arse%22%20-intitle%3A%22arse%7Carses%22amp;f=false">unnumbered page</a>:
<dl><dd>Felnigg. What a suppurating <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></b>. Look at him. <b><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>Arse</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">arses</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">arsing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">arsed</b>)
</p>

<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>Stop</a> <b>arsing</b> around!</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1985</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a> McAughtry, <i>McAughtry's War</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=Pi1nAAAAMAAJamp;q=%22arsing%22+-intitle:%22arse%7Carses%22amp;dq=%22arsing%22+-intitle:%22arse%7Carses%22amp;hl=enamp;ei=OS-5TrDiNqP0mAX59vyCCAamp;sa=Xamp;oi=book_resultamp;ct=resultamp;redir_esc=y">page 10</a>,
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> university material, just <b>arsing</b> about as a rigger, <b>arsing</b> about, killing time with bohunks like <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>.</dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd>Pi, upset, roars, "Quit <b>arsing</b> around there and get cracking," and a dozen heads turn their way.</dd></dl></li>

***artifact.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:artifact.html>artifact</a> (119748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Alteration of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">artefact</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">artefatto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">arte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">by skill</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (ablative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ars</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">art</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">factum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing made</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">facio</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make, do</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:artifact.html>artifact</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">artifacts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An object made or shaped by human hand.</li>
<li>An object made or shaped by some <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> or intelligence, not necessarily of direct human origin.</li>
<li>Something viewed as a product of human agency or conception rather than an inherent element.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Philip Weiss and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>The very act of <a href = vnd.unilang:looking.html>looking</a> at a naked model <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:artifact.html>artifact</a></b> of male supremacy.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2019</b>,  Li Huang |  James <a href = vnd.unilang:lambert.html>Lambert</a>,  “Another Arrow for the Quiver: A New Methodology for Multilingual Researchers”, in  <cite>Journal of Multilingual and Multicultural Development</cite>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" class="extiw" title="w:Digital object identifier">DOI</a>:<span class="neverexpand"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://doi.org/10.1080%2F01434632.2019.1596115">10.1080/01434632.2019.1596115</a></span></small>, page 6:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Overall the signage at <a href = vnd.unilang:nie.html>Nie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> the appearance being a top-down <b>artefact</b> driven by institutional policy with English set as the default language.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A finding or structure in an experiment or investigation that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not a true feature of the object under observation, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a result of external action, the test arrangement, or an experimental error.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The spot on his lung <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> out to be an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:artifact.html>artifact</a></b> of the X-ray process.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaeology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An object, such as a tool, ornament, or weapon of archaeological or historical interest, especially such an object found at an archaeological excavation.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The dig produced many Roman <b>artifacts</b>.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Oliver" class="extiw" title="w:John Oliver">John <a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a></a>,  “North Korea”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Last_Week_Tonight_with_John_Oliver" class="extiw" title="w:Last Week Tonight with John Oliver">Last Week Tonight with John <a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a></a></cite>, season 4, episode 21, written by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tim_Carvell" class="extiw" title="w:Tim Carvell"><a href = vnd.unilang:tim.html>Tim</a> Carvell</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:josh.html>Josh</a> Gondelman; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dan_Gurewitch" class="extiw" title="w:Dan Gurewitch"><a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>Dan</a> Gurewitch</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:jeff.html>Jeff</a> Maurer; <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a> Silva; Will Tracy; <a href = vnd.unilang:jill.html>Jill</a> Twiss; Seena Vali; <a href = vnd.unilang:julie.html>Julie</a> Weiner, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HBO" class="extiw" title="w:HBO">HBO</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Warner_Bros._Television" class="extiw" title="w:Warner Bros. Television">Warner <a href = vnd.unilang:bros.html>Bros</a>. Television</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Holy <a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a>! It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> fascinating when a country’s culture seeps <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> into their math lessons, although it’s not really surprising. As a British child, our math questions <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> “if <a href = vnd.unilang:johnny.html>Johnny</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> two <b>artifacts</b> and Dinesh <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> two <b>artifacts</b>, then how many <b>artifacts</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:johnny.html>Johnny</a> about to have?” The answer, of course, “all the <b>artifacts</b>, Dinesh’s family can come visit them in a British museum whenever they’re in town.”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An appearance or structure in protoplasm due to death, the method of preparation of <a href = vnd.unilang:specimens.html>specimens</a>, or the use of reagents, and not present during life.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A perceptible distortion that appears in an audio or video file or a digital image as a result of applying a lossy compression algorithm.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">This JPEG image <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> so highly compressed that it <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> unsightly compression <b>artifacts</b>, making it unsuitable for the cover of our magazine.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The spelling <i><a href = vnd.unilang:artifact.html>artifact</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> preferred by most American dictionaries, while <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">artefact</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the preferred spelling in Australia’s <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macquarie_Dictionary" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Macquarie Dictionary">Macquarie Dictionary</a></i> with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:artifact.html>artifact</a></i> listed as a variant.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:artikelen.html>artikelen</a> (8113)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:artikelen.html>artikelen</a></strong>
</p>

***artisjok.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:artisjok.html>artisjok</a> (77328)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from Northern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">articiocco</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proven%C3%A7al_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Provençal dialect">Provençal</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="oc">archichaut</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="oc">arquichaut</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Spanish">Old Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osp">alcarchofa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andalusian_Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Andalusian Arabic">Andalusian Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="xaa">اَلْخَرْشُوف</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xaa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">alẖaršúf(a)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">اَلْخُرْشُوف</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">al-ḵuršūf</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, definite form of <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">خُرْشُوف</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ḵuršūf</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:artisjok.html>artisjok</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:artisjokken.html>artisjokken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:artisjok.html>artisjokje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>artichoke, <i>Cynara scolymus</i>, an edible plant related to the thistle <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ersetere</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">arseter</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">arsete</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ercetere</i>. The modern form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> based on or influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Arzt</i>.
